GT Equivalence Verification (BPG5)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4/(c5*P + c6)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: [3, 23, 27, 37, 41]
Matched candidates: ["P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2/(P*c3 + 1) + c4*tanh(c5*t + c6)", "P**2*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3/(P + c4)", "P**2*c0 + P**2*c1*Max(0, P + c2) + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5*Max(0, P + c6) + P*c7/(P*c8 + 1) + c9", "P**2*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5 + P*c6/(P + c7) + c8*exp(c9*t)", "P**2*c0 + P**2*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6 + 1) + c7*tanh(c8*t + c9)"]

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare each candidate to it.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT is:
$$f(P) = 0.9198(1 - P/84.03)P + 0.9198 \cdot P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

Expanding:
$$f(P) = 0.9198P - 0.01095P^2 + 0.9198P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

Key observations:
- GT depends only on P (not on t)
- GT has terms: linear in P, quadratic in P, and a rational term P²/(aP+1)
- The rational term P²/(aP+1) can be rewritten: P²/(aP+1) = (P/a) - (P/a)/(aP+1) = P/a - 1/(a²) + 1/(a²(aP+1))... or alternatively P·c/(cP+1) form.

Let me rewrite the rational part: $\frac{P^2}{7.531P+1}$. This equals $P \cdot \frac{P}{7.531P+1}$, which is a P times a rational function.

So GT = $\alpha P^2 + \beta P + \gamma \frac{P^2}{cP+1}$ where $\alpha = -0.01095$, $\beta = 0.9198$, $\gamma = 0.9198$, $c = 7.531$.

Alternatively: GT = $\alpha P^2 + \beta P + \gamma P \cdot \frac{P}{cP+1}$

Note that $\frac{P}{cP+1}$ is NOT the same as $\frac{P}{P+d}$ (they differ by scaling). Actually $\frac{P}{cP+1} = \frac{1}{c} \cdot \frac{P}{P+1/c}$, so $\frac{P^2}{cP+1} = \frac{P^2}{c(P+1/c)}$.

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P + c_2 P + c_3$
This simplifies to $aP^2 + bP + c_3$. This is a polynomial. GT has a rational term that cannot be represented as a polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 2: Contains Max functions. For specific ranges of P, Max(0, P+c) behaves differently. This is piecewise, not equivalent to a smooth rational function for all P ≥ 0. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 3: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P + c_2 \frac{P}{c_3 P + 1} + c_4 \tanh(c_5 t + c_6)$

Set $c_4 = 0$ to eliminate the tanh term. Then: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P + \frac{c_2 P}{c_3 P + 1}$.

Now compare with GT: $\alpha P^2 + \beta P + \gamma \frac{P^2}{cP+1}$.

The rational term in candidate 3 is $\frac{c_2 P}{c_3 P + 1}$, but GT has $\frac{\gamma P^2}{cP+1}$. These differ by a factor of P. Can we reconcile?

Let me find a common denominator for the GT:
$$\frac{\alpha P^2(cP+1) + \beta P(cP+1) + \gamma P^2}{cP+1} = \frac{(\alpha c)P^3 + (\alpha + \beta c + \gamma)P^2 + \beta P}{cP+1}$$

For candidate 3 (with tanh zeroed):
$$\frac{c_0 P^2(c_3 P+1) + c_1 P(c_3 P+1) + c_2 P}{c_3 P+1} = \frac{c_0 c_3 P^3 + (c_0 + c_1 c_3)P^2 + (c_1 + c_2)P}{c_3 P+1}$$

Matching coefficients with $c_3 = c$ (GT's 7.531):
- $P^3$: $c_0 \cdot c_3 = \alpha \cdot c$ → $c_0 = \alpha = -0.01095$ ✓
- $P^2$: $c_0 + c_1 c_3 = \alpha + \beta c + \gamma$ → $c_1 c_3 = \beta c + \gamma$ → $c_1 = \beta + \gamma/c$
- $P^1$: $c_1 + c_2 = \beta$ → $c_2 = \beta - c_1 = -\gamma/c$
- $P^0$: 0 = 0 ✓

All coefficients can be matched! **MATCH**

### Candidate 4: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 + c_2 P + P^{c_3} c_4 \exp(c_5 t) + c_6 \tanh(c_7 t + c_8) + c_9$

Setting $c_4 = 0, c_6 = 0, c_9 = 0$: becomes $aP^2 + bP$. Missing rational term. **NO MATCH**

But wait - if $c_5 = 0$, then $P^{c_3} c_4 \exp(0) = c_4 P^{c_3}$. With $c_3 = 2$, this gives another $P^2$ term. Still polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 5: Contains Max. Setting $c_3 = 0, c_5 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 6: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 = aP^2 + bP + c$. Polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 7: Contains Max functions. Piecewise. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 8: $aP^2 + bP + c$. Polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 9: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 + c_2 P^2 + c_3 P + c_4 P + c_5 \tanh(c_6 t + c_7) + c_8$. Set $c_5 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 10: Contains Max and tanh(t). Setting $c_3 = 0, c_4 = 0, c_7 = 0$: polynomial + Max. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 11: $aP^2 + bP + c_5 \exp(c_6 t)$. Has t-dependence that can't be zeroed without losing everything non-polynomial. Set $c_5 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 12: Contains $P c_3/|P^5| = c_3/P^4$ (for P>0), $\exp(c_2 t)$, $t\exp(c_7 t)$. Setting t-dependent terms to 0 and $c_3 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 13: Set $c_3 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 14: Set $c_3 = 0, c_6 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 15: Contains $P^{c_3} c_4 \exp(Pc_5)$ and Max. The exponential in P makes this non-polynomial/non-rational unless $c_4 = 0$ and $c_7 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 16: Has tanh(t) terms. Setting those to 0 leaves polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 17: Set t-terms to 0: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 18: Contains Max and exp(t). **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 19: Set $c_2 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 20: Contains log, Max, exp(t). Complex. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 21: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 P \log(1 + c_4/P) + c_5 P + c_6 P + c_7 t/(c_8 + t^2)$

Set $c_7 = 0$. Then: $aP^2 + bP + c_3 P \log(1 + c_4/P)$.

Now $P\log(1 + c_4/P)$ is NOT equivalent to $P^2/(cP+1)$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 22: Contains exp(t), $P c_4/|P^2| = c_4/P$ (for P>0). Setting t-terms to 0: $aP^2 + bP + c_4/P$. Not matching rational form. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 23: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 + c_2 P + \frac{c_3 P}{P + c_4}$

This is: $aP^2 + bP + \frac{c_3 P}{P + c_4}$

Compare with GT: $\alpha P^2 + \beta P + \gamma \frac{P^2}{cP+1}$

Common denominator for GT (using $P + 1/c$):
$$\frac{\alpha P^2(P+1/c) + \beta P(P+1/c) + (\gamma/c) P^2}{P+1/c}$$

For candidate 23:
$$\frac{a P^2(P+c_4) + bP(P+c_4) + c_3 P}{P+c_4}$$
$$= \frac{aP^3 + (ac_4+b)P^2 + (bc_4+c_3)P}{P+c_4}$$

GT over common denominator (with $d = 1/c$):
$$\frac{\alpha P^3 + (\alpha d + \beta + \gamma/c)P^2 + \beta d \cdot P}{P+d}$$
$$= \frac{\alpha P^3 + (\alpha/c + \beta + \gamma/c)P^2 + (\beta/c) P}{P+1/c}$$

Matching: $c_4 = 1/c = d$, $a = \alpha$, $ac_4 + b = \alpha/c + \beta + \gamma/c$, so $b = \beta + \gamma/c$, and $bc_4 + c_3 = \beta/c$, so $c_3 = \beta/c - bc_4 = \beta/c - (\beta + \gamma/c)/c = \beta/c - \beta/c - \gamma/c^2 = -\gamma/c^2$.

All coefficients determined consistently! **MATCH**

### Candidate 24: Contains $\exp(Pc_5)$ and $\sin(c_7 t)$. Setting $c_4 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 25: Contains $t/(c_3+t^2)$ and $\sin(c_6 t)$. t-dependent. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 26: Contains $P c_3 \exp(Pc_4)$ and $t\exp(c_7 t)$. Setting $c_3 = 0, c_6 = 0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 27: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 \text{Max}(0,P+c_2) + (c_3+c_4)P + c_5 P \text{Max}(0,P+c_6) + \frac{c_7 P}{c_8 P+1} + c_9$

Setting Max coefficients $c_1 = 0, c_5 = 0, c_9 = 0$: $aP^2 + bP + \frac{c_7 P}{c_8 P + 1}$

Same structure as Candidate 23 analysis (with $\frac{c_7 P}{c_8 P+1} = \frac{(c_7/c_8)P}{P+1/c_8}$). By the same argument as Candidate 23, this **MATCH**es.

### Candidates 28-50: Let me check the remaining ones quickly for the key structure $P^2 + P + P^2/(cP+1)$ or equivalent.

### Candidate 28-50: Most are polynomials + exp(t) or tanh(t) or Max or other non-rational terms. Setting those to zero leaves polynomials.

### Candidate 37: $aP^2 + bP + \frac{c_6 P}{P+c_7} + c_8 \exp(c_9 t)$. Set $c_8 = 0$: same as Candidate 23 structure. **MATCH**

### Candidate 41: $c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2 \exp(c_2 t) + (c_3+c_4)P + \frac{c_5 P}{c_6 P+1} + c_7 \tanh(c_8 t+c_9)$. Set $c_1=0, c_7=0$: $aP^2 + bP + \frac{c_5 P}{c_6 P+1}$. **MATCH**
